//   :TITLE Sahidica
//    Sahidica 2.01 (2007.January.28)
//   ===========================================================================
//    IMPORTANT NOTE: 
//    This text is best viewed in Wordpad(R) with View/Options set to No wrap.
//   ===========================================================================
//    "Sahidica - A New Edition of the New Testament in Sahidic Coptic"
//    Copyright (c)2000-2007 by J Warren Wells. All rights reserved.
//   
//    For more information visit www.sahidica.org.
//   
//    This edition is available free of charge for use in free electronic 
//    editions of the New Testament as long as the full title and copyright 
//    information are included and credited. For written permission to use 
//    all or any part of this document in print editions, contact the editor
//    at www.sahidica.org.
//   
//    This edition is primarily meant for use by teachers and students of
//    Sahidic Coptic, and to a lesser degree by Coptologists involved in
//    scholarly research, textual criticism, or New Testament translation.
//   ===========================================================================
//   :ENCODING
//   ===========================================================================
//    Character representation in the Greek and Coptic texts.
//    (These characters are mapped in the UncialSS font, which 
//    is freely available on the www.sahidica.org website.)
//   ------------------------------------------------------------------------
//    a alpha    i iota     r rho      S shai
//    b beta     k kappa    s sigma*   F fai
//    g gamma    l lambda   t tau      H hori
//    d delta    m mu       u upsilon  J janjia
//    e epsilon  n nu       f phi      C chima
//    z zeta     x xi       c khi      T ti
//    h eta      o omicron  y psi      Q chi (Bo)*
//    q theta    p pi       w omega    X stauros *
//   ------------------------------------------------------------------------
//    * Neither "chi" (Bohairic) nor "stauros" are used in Sahidica 
//    V is reserved for final Greek sigma. 
//    A is reserved for Achmimic hori.
//   ------------------------------------------------------------------------
//    Font: The UncialSS (Uncial Sans Serif) Font was developed to allow 
//    easy comparison of parallel Coptic and Greek texts. It emulates the 
//    script found in both Coptic and Greek Uncial manuscripts.
//   ------------------------------------------------------------------------
//    Sections and Paragraphs: Following each book-ch-vs, there may appear
//    encoding: where "=" is a section break, and "-" is a paragraph break.
//    These are aligned, but not identical, to those found in the UBS text
//    where section headings appear.
//   ===========================================================================
//   :PURPOSE
//   ===========================================================================
//    Please note: This text is a work in progress. As such, there 
//    is an ongoing effort to standardize the spelling of words in 
//    the text. Be aware that version updates periodically appear.
//   
//    The primary purpose is to produce a standardized edition of
//    the Sahidic NT similar to standard Greek editions.
//   
//    An additional purpose of this text is to allow side-by-side
//    comparison with the Greek New Testament. To facilitate this
//    effort, a new version of the Greek text has been developed,
//    which is meant to better represent the Greek text upon which
//    the Sahidic was based. This text is entitled "The New Testament
//    According to the Egyptian Greek Text" [NTAEG]
//   
//    This text does not include representation of either accents or 
//    supralinear strokes, since these are used inconsistently in the 
//    original texts. There is also a higher degree of standardization
//    in spelling and punctuation; like today's standard Greek master
//    texts, but unlike both the original Sahidic texts, and the PHI
//    and Coptic Society texts. Moreover, as in standard Greek texts,
//    instances of the Nomina Sacra have been expanded to their full
//    forms. This is again a departure from earlier versions of the
//    Sahidic, including the PHI and Coptic Society texts, which are
//    Both inconsistent in their usage.
//    
//    Special thanks to David Brakke of Indiana University Bloomington, 
//    Brigitte Comparini of the Packard Humanities Institute, and
//    Michael Heiser, Academic Editor, at Logos Research Systems; for
//    their assistance in making this edition possible.
//    
//   ===========================================================================
//   :BASIS
//   ===========================================================================
//    Sahidica was initially based (by permission) on the Coptic New Testament, 
//    which is an electronic publication, which was edited by David Brakke. 
//    (PHI-CD 5.3 dated 7/2/91. Los Altos. Packard Humanities Institute. 1991).
//   
//    During later development, Sahidica was electronically collated against 
//    the Coptic CD I by the St. Shenouda The Archmandrite Coptic Society.
//    Los Angeles, CA dated April, 1998.
//   
//    These two editions were reduced to a raw electronic form, which allowed both
//    to be compared electronically letter by letter with Sahidica in order to
//    accurately detect and report every single variation and input error in any
//    of the texts. Though errors are inevitable, the collators of three seperate
//    editions are highly unlikely to make the same errors. Therefore, this method
//    helps to insure the integrity of the Sahidica edition.
//   
//    Throughout the project, Sahidica was also collated against printed editions
//    of the following coptic manuscripts, which manuscripts date from the third 
//    century and later.
//   --------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
//    Matt:  Pierpont Morgan Library M-569 collated against Bodmer XIX papyrus
//    Mark:* PPalau Rib. Inv.Nr.182 collated against Pierpont Morgan Library M-569
//    Luke:  PPalau Rib. Inv.Nr.181 collated against Pierpont Morgan Library M-569
//    John:  PPalau Rib. Inv.Nr.183 collated against Pierpont Morgan Library M-569
//    Acts:  Chester Beatty B (Copt.Ms.814) collated against Berlin P.15926 and British Museum MS Or.7594
//    Paul:  Chester Beatty A (Copt.Ms.813) collated against Pierpont Morgan Library M-570 and M-571
//    James-Jude:** Pierpont Morgan Library M-572 collated against the Pierpont Morgan Library M-573 and M-601***
//    Revelation: Berlin MS Or.408 ( British Museum Ms Or.3518) collated against British Museum MS Or.6803
//   ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
//      * Note: The longer and shorter endings of Mark are based on Horner; cf Kahle (JTS.1951.p49-57)
//     ** Note: 1st Peter was also collated against the Crosby-Schøyen Ms.193.
//    *** Note: Portions of James and Jude were reconstructed from M-573, M-601, and four other mss. 
//   ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
//    Note on Interpolations 
//    The short and long endings of Mark are ommited from the PPalau ms 182, but they do appear in most mss.
//    To better represent the overall Sahidic tradition, both endings are included, but in double brackets.
//    The pericope of the adultress (John 7:53-8:11) does not appear in any Sahidic ms. Herein it is omitted.
//   ===========================================================================
//   book-ch-vs "=" is section break, "-" is paragraph
//   ===========================================================================
//   Prepared (with permission) for use with BibleWorks by Jim Darlack.
//   August 2007 (http://bibleworks.oldinthenew.org)
//
mat 1:1 = pJwwme mpeJpo nihsous pecristos pShre ndaueid pShre nabraHam.
mat 1:2 - abraHam aFJpo nisaak isaak de aFJpo niakwb iakwb de aFJpo nioudas mn neFsnhu.
mat 1:3 ioudas de aFJpo mfares mn zara ebol Hn qamar fares de aFJpo nesrwm. esrwm de aFJpo naram.
mat 1:4 aram de aFJpo naminadab. aminadab de aFJpo nnaasswn naasswn de aFJpo nsalmwn.
mat 1:5 salmwn de aFJpo nboes ebol Hn Hracab. boes de aFJpo niwbhd ebol Hn Hrouq. iwbhd de aFJpo niessai.
mat 1:6 - iessai de aFJpo ndaueid prro. daueid de aFJpo nsolomwn ebol Hn qime nourias.
mat 1:7 solomwn de aFJpo nHroboam Hroboam de aFJpo nabia abias de aFJpo nasaf.
mat 1:8 asaf de aFJpo niwsafat iwsafat de aFJpo niwram iwram de aFJpo nozeias.
mat 1:9 ozeias de aFJpo niwaqam. iwnaqam de aFJpo nacaz acaz de aFJpo nezekeias.
mat 1:10 ezekeias de aFJpo mmanassh manassh de aFJpo nHamws. Hamws de aFJpo niwsias.
mat 1:11 iwsias de aFJpo nieconias mn neFsnhu Hi ppwwne ebol ntbabulwn.
mat 1:12 - mnnsa ppwwne de ebol ntbabulwn ieconias aFJpo nsalaqihl salaqihl de aFJpo nzorobabel.
mat 1:13 zorobabel de aFJpo nabioud abioud de aFJpo neliakim. eliakim de aFJpo nazwra.
mat 1:14 azwras de aFJpo nsadwk sadwk de aFJpo naceim aceim de aFJpo nelioud.
mat 1:15 elioud de aFJpo neleazar eleazar de aFJpo mmatqam matqam de aFJpo niakwb.
mat 1:16 iakwb de aFJpo niwshf pHai mmaria. tai ntauJpe ihsous ebol nHhts. pai nSaumoute eroF Je pecristos.
mat 1:17 = genea Ce nim Jin abraHam Sa eHrai edaueid mn taFte ngenea. auw Jin daueid SaeHrai eppwwne ebol ntbabulwn mn taFte ngenea. auw Jin eppwwne ebol ntbabulwn SaeHrai epecristos mn taFte ngenea.
mat 1:18 peJpo de nihsous pecristos neuteiHe pe nterouSp toots nteFmaau maria niwshf empatoubwk eHoun Saneuerhu auHe eros eseet ebol Hn oupna eFouaab.
mat 1:19 iwshf de pesHai eneudikaios pe. auw neFouwS an eT mpessoeit aFouwS enoJs ebol nJioue.
mat 1:20 nai de ntereFmeeue eroou eis paggelos mpJoeis aFouwnH naF ebol Hn ourasou eFJw mmos Je iwshf pShre ndaueid mprro Hote eJi mmaria teksHime. petounaJpoF gar ebol nHhts ouebol Hn oupneuma eFouaab pe.
mat 1:21 snaJpo de nouShre. ngmoute epeFran Je ihsous. ntoF gar petnatouJo mpeFlaos ebol Hn neunobe.
mat 1:22 pai de thrF ntaFSwpe Jekaas eFeJwk ebol nCi pentapJoeis JooF Hitm peprofhths eFJw mmos.
mat 1:23 Je eistparqenos naw nsJpo nouShre nsemoute epeFran Je emmanouhl ete pai pe nSauouaHmeF Je pnoute nmman.
mat 1:24 aFtwoun de nCi iwshf eFnkotk aFeire kata qe ntaFHwn etootF nCi paggelos mpJoeis. aFJi mmaria teFsHime.
mat 1:25 mpeFsouwns SantesJpo mpesShre. aFmoute epeFran Je ihsous.
mat 2:1 = ihsous de nterouJpoF Hrai Hn bhqleem nte Toudaia Hn neHoou nHhrwdhs prro. eis Henmagos auei ebol Hn nemanSa eHrai eqierosoluma. euJw mmos.
mat 2:2 Je eFtwn prro nnioudai ntauJpoF. annau gar epeFsiou Hn nemanSa anei eouwSt naF.
mat 2:3 aFswtm de nCi Hhrwdhs prro. aFStortr emate mn qierosoluma thrs nmmaF.
mat 2:4 aFswouH eHoun nnarciereus throu mn negrammateus mplaos. aFSine ebol Hitootou Je eunaJpo mpecristos twn.
mat 2:5 ntoou de peJau naF Je Hrai Hn bhqleem nteToudaia. eFshH gar nteiHe Hitm peprofhths.
mat 2:6 Je nto Hwwte bhqleem pkaH niouda nteJolH an Hn nHhgemwn niouda. Fnhu gar ebol nHhte nCi ouHhgoumenos. pai etnamoone mpalaos pisrahl.
mat 2:7 - tote Hhrwdhs aFmoute emmagos nJioue aFSine ebol Hitootou nsapeuoeiS mpsiou ntaFouwnH ebol.
mat 2:8 aFJoose eHrai ebhqleem eFJw mmos Je bwk ntetn Sine Hn ouwrJ etbe pShre Shm. eSwpe de etetnSanHe eroF matammoi Hw Jekaas eieei ntaouwSt naF.
mat 2:9 ntoou de nterouswtm ebol Hitm prro aubwk auw eispsiou ntaunau eroF Hn nemanSa aFmooSe Hhtou SanteFei nFaHeratF eJm pma enerepShre Shm nHhtF.
mat 2:10 nterounau epsiou auraSe Hn ounoC nraSe emate.
mat 2:11 auw nterouei eHrai ephi aunau epShre Shm mn maria teFmaau aupaHtou auouwSt naF auouwn nneuaHwwr aueine naF nHendwron ounoub mn oulibanos mn ouSal.
mat 2:12 autouneiatou de ebol Hn ourasou etmkotou SaHhrwdhs. ebol Hitn keHih auanacwrei eHrai eteucora.
mat 2:13 = nteroubwk de eispaggelos mpJoeis aFouwnH ebol Hn ourasou eiwshf eFJw mmos Je twoun ngJi mpShre Shm mn teFmaau ngbwk eHrai ekhme ngSwpe Hm pma etmmau SanTJoos nak. Hhrwdhs gar naSine nsapShre Shm etakoF.
mat 2:14 ntoF de aFtwoun aFJi mpShre Shm mn teFmaau nteuSh aFbwk eHrai ekhme.
mat 2:15 neFSoop de Hm pma etmmau SanteHhrwdhs mou. Jekaas eFeJwk ebol nCi pentapJoeis JooF Hitm peprofhths eFJw mmos Je aimoute epaShre ebol Hn khme.
mat 2:16 = tote Hhrwdhs ntereFnau Je auswbe mmoF ebol Hitn mmagos aFCwnt emate aFJoou aFmouout nShre Shm nim etHn bhqleem mn netSoop Hn nestoS throu Jinrmpe snte epesht. katapeuoeiS ntauHetHwtF ebol Hitootou nmmagos.
mat 2:17 tote aFJwk ebol nCi pentauJooF Hitn ierhmias peprofhths eFJw mmos.
mat 2:18 Je ousmh auswtm eros Hn Hramma. ourime mnoutoeit enaSwF. Hrachl esrime enesShre auw mpesouwS eslswls Je nnous an ne.
mat 2:19 = ntereFmou de nCi Hhrwdhs. eispaggelos mpJoeis aFouwnH ebol Hn ourasou eiwshf Hn khme.
mat 2:20 eFJw mmos Je twoun ngJi mpShre Shm mn teFmaau ngbwk eHrai epkaH mpisrahl. aumou gar nCi netSine nsateyuch mpShre Shm.
mat 2:21 ntoF de aFtwoun aFJi mpShre Shm mn teFmaau aFbwk eHrai epkaH mpisrahl.
mat 2:22 aFswtm de Je archlaos peto nrro eJn Toudaia epma nHhrwdhs peFeiwt aFrHote ebwk epma etmmau. autouneiatF de ebol Hn ourasou aFanacwrei eHrai emmooSte ntgalilaia.
mat 2:23 aFei aFouwH Hn oupolis nSaumoute eros Je nazareq. Jekaas eFeJwk ebol nCi pentauJooF Hitm peprofhths Je senamoute eroF Je pnazwraios.
mat 3:1 = Hrai de Hn neHoou etmmau aFei nCi iwHannhs pbaptisths eFtaSeoeiS Hrai Hm pJaie nToudaia
mat 3:2 eFJw mmos Je metanoi. asHwn gar eHoun nCi tmntrro nmphue.
mat 3:3 pai gar pentauJooF Hitn hsaias peprofhths eFJw mmos Je tesmh mpetwS ebol Hi pJaie Je sbteteHih mpJoeis ntetn sooutn nneFma nmooSe.
mat 3:4 ntoF de iwHannhs nereteFHbsw Soop ebol Hn Henbw nCamoul. ereoumoJH nSaar Coole eteFTpe. teFHre de neHenSJe ne mnouebie Hoout.
mat 3:5 tote nesnhu ebol eratF nCi qierosoluma thrs. mn Toudaia mn tpericwros thrs mpeiordanhs.
mat 3:6 euJi baptisma ebol HitootF Hm peiordanhs peiero euexomologei nneunobe.
mat 3:7 - ntereFnau de eHaH Hn nefarissaios mn nsaddoukaios eunhu eJm pbaptisma peJaF nau. Je neJpo nneHboui. nim pentaFtsabe thutn epwt ebol Hhts ntorgh etnhu.
mat 3:8 arire Ce noukarpos eFmpSa ntmetanoia.
mat 3:9 ntetn tmmeeue eJoos nHhtthutn. Je ountan mmau mpeneiwt abraHam. TJw gar mmos nhtn Je ounCom mpnoute etounes HenShre nabraHam ebol Hn neiwne.
mat 3:10 Jintenou de pkelebin kh Ha tnoune nnShn. Shn Ce nim etenFnaeire an noukarpos enanouF senakooreF nsenoJF etsate.
mat 3:11 anok men eibaptize mmwtn Hn oumoou eumetanoia. petnhu de FJoor eroi pai nTmpSa an nFi Ha peFtooue. ntoF petnabaptize mmwtn Hn oupna eFouaab mnousate.
mat 3:12 pai etere peFHa Hn teFCiJ eFnatbbo mpeFJnoou. nFswouH eHoun mpeFsouo etapoqhkh. ptwH de nFrokHF Hn ousate emeswSm.
mat 3:13 = tote aFei nCi ihsous ebol Hn tgalilaia eHrai eJm piordanhs SaiwHannhs etreFbaptize ebol HitootF.
mat 3:14 ntoF de aFkwlu mmoF eFJw mmos Je anok etrcria nbaptize ebol Hi tootk auw ntok etnhu Saroi.
mat 3:15 auouwSb de nCi ihsous eFJw mmos naF Je Cw tenou tai gar te qe eteSSe eron eJwk ebol ndikaiosunh nim tote aFkaaF.
mat 3:16 ntereFbaptize Ce nCi ihsous nteunou aFei eHrai Hm pmoou. auw eis Hhhte auouwn nCi mphue. aFnau epepneuma mpnoute eFnhu epesht nqe nouCroompe eHrai eJwF.
mat 3:17 auw eis Hhhte eisousmh ebol Hn mphue esJw mmos Je pai pe paShre pamerit pentapaouwS Swpe Hrai nHhtF.
mat 4:1 = tote ihsous auJitF eHrai eterhmos ebol Hitm pepneuma etreupeiraze mmoF ebol Hitm pdiabolos.
mat 4:2 aFnhsteue de nHme nHoou mn Hme nouSh mnnsws aFHko.
mat 4:3 aFTpeFouoi eroF nCi petpeiraze peJaF naF. Je eSJe ntok pe pShre mpnoute aJis Jekaas ere neiwne roeik.
mat 4:4 ntoF de aFouwSb eFJw mmos Je FshH Je nereprwme nawnH an eoeik mauaaF alla eSaJe nim etnhu ebol Hn ttapro mpnoute.
mat 4:5 tote aFJi mmoF nCi pdiabolos eHrai etpolis etouaab. aFtaHo mmoF eratF eJm pthnH mprpe.
mat 4:6 peJaF naF Je eSJe ntok pe pShre mpnoute noJk epesht eJm peima. FshH gar Je FnaHwn etootou nneFaggelos etbhhtk. nseFi mmok eHrai eJn neuCiJ mhpote ngJwrp euwne ntekouerhte.
mat 4:7 peJaF on nCi ihsous Je FshH on Je nnekpeiraze mpJoeis peknoute.
mat 4:8 palin on aFJitF nCi pdiabolos eHrai eJn outoou eFJose emate. aFtouoF emmntrrwou throu mpkosmos mn peueoou.
mat 4:9 peJaF naF. Je nai throu Tnataau nak ekSanpaHtk ngouwSt nai.
mat 4:10 tote peJaF naF nCi ihsous Je bwk psatanas. FshH gar Je pJoeis peknoute petkeouwSt naF. auw ntoF mauaaF petkeSmSe naF.
mat 4:11 tote aFkaaF nCi pdiabolos. auw eis Hhhte eisnaggelos auei audiakonei naF.
mat 4:12 = aFswtm de Je auparadidou niwHannhs aFanacwrei eHrai etgalilaia.
mat 4:13 aFkw nswF nnazareq. aFei aFouwH Hn kaparnaoum. tai etHatn qalassa Hn ntoS nzaboulwn mn nefqaleim.
mat 4:14 Jekaas eFeJwk ebol nCi pentauJooF Hitn hsaias peprofhths eFJw mmos.
mat 4:15 Je pkaH nzaboulwn pkaH nefqaleim. teHih nqalassa pekro mpeiordanhs. tgalilaia nnHeqnos.
mat 4:16 plaos etHmoos Hm pkake aFnau eunoC nouoein. netouhH Hn tecwra mn qaibes mpmou pouoein aFSa nau.
mat 4:17 - JinpeuoeiS etmmau aFarcei nCi ihsous etaSeoeiS aFw eJoos. Je metanoei asHwn gar eHoun nCi tmntrro nmphue.
mat 4:18 = eFmooSe de Hatn qalassa ntgalilaia aFnau eson snau. simwn pete Saumoute eroF Je petros mn andreas peFson euHiSne eHrai eqalassa Je neHenouwHe gar ne.
mat 4:19 peJaF nau Je amhitn oueHthutn nswi. tarthutn nouwHe nrwme.
mat 4:20 ntoou de nteunou aukw nneuSnhu. auouaHou nswF.
mat 4:21 aFmooSe de on eqh nkekoui. aFnau ekeson snau iakwbos pShre nzebedaios mn iwHannhs peFson Hrai Hm pJoi mn zebedaios peueiwt eusoFte nneuSnhu aFmoute eroou.
mat 4:22 ntoou de nteunou aukw nneuSnhu mn peueiwt auouaHou nswF.
mat 4:23 = aFei de ebol Hn tgalilaia thrs eFTsbw Hrai Hn neusunagwgh auw eFtaSeoeiS mpeuaggelion ntmntrro eFrpaHre eSwne nim HiloJlJ nim etHm plaos.
mat 4:24 peFsoeit aFbwk ebol Hn tsuria thrs aueine naF nouon nim etmokH Hn HenSwne euSobe auw euSoop Hn Hentkas mn neto ndaimwnion mn netHite mn netshC aFrpaHre eroou.
mat 4:25 auw auouaHou nswF nCi HenmhhSe enaSwou ebol Hn tgalilaia mn tdekapolis mn qierosoluma mn Toudaia mn pekro mpeiordanhs .
mat 5:1 = ntereFnau de emmhhSe aFale eHrai eJm ptoou. auw ntereFHmoos auTpeuouoi eroF nCi neFmaqhths.
mat 5:2 aFouwn erwF aFTsbw nau eFJw mmos.
mat 5:3 Je naiatou nnHhke Hm pepneuma Je twou te tmntrro nmphue.
mat 5:4 naiatou nnetrHbbe Je ntoou netounaspswpou.
mat 5:5 naiatou nnrmraS Je ntoou netnaklhronomei mpkaH.
mat 5:6 naiatou nnetHkaeit etobe ntdikaiosunh Je ntoou netnasei.
mat 5:7 naiatou nnnaht Je ntoou netounana nau.
mat 5:8 naiatou nnetouaab Hm peuHht Je ntoou netnanau epnoute.
mat 5:9 naiatou nnreFreirhnh Je ntoou netounamoute eroou Je nShre mpnoute.
mat 5:10 naiatou nntaupwt nswou etbe tdikaiosunh Je twou te tmntrro nmphue.
mat 5:11 naiatthutn euSanneCneCthutn. nsepwt nswtn. nseJeHwb nim eqoou eHoun erwtn euJiCol erwtn etbhht.
mat 5:12 raSe ntetn telhl Je petnbeke naSwF Hrai Hn mphue. tai gar te qe ntaupwt nsaneprofhths etHatetnHh.
mat 5:13 = ntwtn pe peHmou mpkaH erSanpeHmou de baabe eunamolHF nou. meFrSau nlaau nsanoJF ebol nseHomF Hitn nerwme.
mat 5:14 ntwtn pe pouoein mpkosmos. mn SCom noupolis eHwp eskh eHrai HiJn outoou.
mat 5:15 oude meuJereouHhbs nsekaaF HaouSi. alla nSaukaaF HiJn tlucnia nFrouoein enetSoop throu Hm phi.
mat 5:16 tai te qe mareFrouoein nCi petnouoen mpemto ebol nnerwme Jekaas euenau enetnHbhue etnanouou nseTeoou mpetneiwt etHn mphue.
mat 5:17 = mprwS Je ntaiei ekatalu mpnomos hneprofhths. ntaiei an ekatalu mmoou alla eJokou ebol.
mat 5:18 Hamhn gar TJw mmos nhtn. Je Santetpe parage mn pkaH ouiwta nouwt. houSwlH nouwt nneuseine ebol Hm pnomos SantouSwpe throu.
mat 5:19 petnabwl Ce ebol nouei nneientolh etsobk nFTsbw nnrwme nteiHe senamoute eroF Je pelacistos Hn tmntrro nmphue petnaaau de auw nFTsbw nHhtou pai senamoute eroF Je pnoC Hn tmntrro mpnoute.
mat 5:20 TJw gar mmos nhtn. Je esSantmrHouo nCi tetndikaiosunh nHouo eta negrammateus mn nefarissaios nnetnbwk eHoun etmntrro nmphue.
mat 5:21 = atetnswtm Je auJoos nnarcaios Je nnekHwtb. petnaHwtb de Fo nenocos etekrisis.
mat 5:22 anok de TJw mmos nhtn Je ouon nim etnanouCs epeFson eikh Fo nenocos etekrisis. petnaJoos mpeFson Je kSoueit Fo nenocos epsunHedrion. petnaJoos Je psoC Fo nenocos etgeHenna nsate.
mat 5:23 eSwpe de ekSanei eknatalo mpekdwron eHrai eJm pequsiasthrion. ngrpmeeue mpma etmmau Je ountepekson ouHwb eHoun erok.

mat 25:31 = Hotan de eFSanei nCi pShre mprwme Hrai Hm peFeoou mn neFaggelos throu nmmaF. tote FnaHmoos eJm peqronos mpeFeoou.
mat 25:32 nseswouH eHoun mpeFmto ebol nnHeqnos throu nFpwrJ mmoou ebol nneuerhu nqe nouSws nSaFpwrJ nnesoou ebol nnbaampe.
mat 25:33 nesoou men nFtaHoou eratou Hiounam mmoF. nbaampe de HiHbour mmoF.
mat 25:34 tote FnaJoos nCi prro nnetHiounam mmoF. Je amhitn netsmamaat ntepaeiwt. ntetn klhronomei ntmntrro ntausbtwts nhtn Jinetkatabolh mpkosmos.
mat 25:35 aiHko gar atetntmoi. aieibe atetntsoi. neio nSmmo pe atetnSopt erwtn.
mat 25:36 neikh kaHhu atetnT Hiwwt. neiSwne atetnCm paSine. neiHmpeSteko pe atetnei Saroi.
mat 25:37 tote senaouwSb naF nCi ndikaios euJw mmos Je pJoeis ntannau erok tnau ekHkaeit antmmok. hekobe antsok.

mat 25:39 ntannau de erok tnau ekSwne. hekHm peSteko anei Sarok.
mat 25:40 FnaouwSb de nCi prro nFJoos nau Je Hamhn TJw mmos nhtn. Je efoson atetnaas noua nneisnhu etsobk ntatetnaas nai.
mat 25:41 - tote FnaouwSb nFJoos nnkooue etHiHbour mmoF. Je saHethutn ebol mmoi netsHouort etsate nSa eneH ntausbtwts mpdiabolos mn neFaggelos.
mat 25:42 aiHko gar mpetntmoi. aieibe mpetntsoi.

mat 26:1 = asSwpe de ntere ihsous ouw nneiSaJe throu. peJaF nneFmaqhths.

mat 28:1 = rouHe de mpsabbaton eHtooue nsoua mpsabbaton. asei nCi maria tmagdalhnh mn tkemaria enau eptafos.
mat 28:2 auw eis Hhhte eisounoC nkmto aFSwpe. paggelos gar mpJoeis aFei epesht Hn tpe aFTpeFouoi aFskorkr mpwne. aFHmoos eHrai eJwF.
mat 28:3 peFeine de neFo nqe nouebrhCe auw teFHbsw nesouobS nqe nouciwn.
mat 28:4 ebol de Hn teFHote aunoein nCi netHareH. auSwpe nqe nnetmoout.
mat 28:5 aFouwSb de nCi paggelos peJaF nneHiome Je ntwtn mprrHote. Tsooun gar Je etetnSine nsaihsous pentaustaurou mmoF.
mat 28:6 nFmpeima an aFtwoun gar kata qe ntaFJoos. amhitn ntetnnau epma eneFnHhtF.
mat 28:7 auw ntetnbwk Hn ouCeph ntetnJoos nneFmaqhths Je aFtwoun ebol Hn netmoout. auw eis Hhhte FnarSorp erwtn etgalilaia etetnanau eroF Hm pma etmmau. eis Hhhte aiJoos nhtn.
mat 28:8 aubwk Hn ouCeph ebol Hm pemHaau aupwt Hn ouHote mnounoC nraSe eJipouw nneFmaqhths.
mat 28:9 auw eis Hhhte eihsousis aFtwmnt eroou eFJw mmos Je cairaite. ntoou de auTpeuouoi auamaHte nneFouerhte auouwSt naF.
mat 28:10 peJaF nau nCi ihsous Je mprrHote bwk ntetnJipouw nnasnhu Jekaas eunabwk eHrai etgalilaia eunanau gar eroi Hm pma etmmau.
mat 28:11 = ntoou de eubhk eisHoine ntkoustwdia aubwk eHoun etpolis auJipouw nnarciereus nnentauSwpe throu.
mat 28:12 auswouH de eHoun nnepresbuteros. auJi nouSoJne auT nHnnoC nHomnt nmmatoi.
mat 28:13 euJw mmos Je aJis Je neFmaqhths nentauei nteuSh auFitF nJioue ennkotk.
mat 28:14 eSwpe de euSansetmpai nCi pHhgemwn anon tnnapeiqe mmoF ntnrthutn natroouS.
mat 28:15 ntoou de nterouJi nnHomnt aueire kata qe ntauTsbw nau. peiSaJe aFTsoeit Hn nioudai SaeHrai epoou nHoou.
mat 28:16 = pmntoue de mmaqhths aubwk eHrai etgalilaia eHrai eptoou ntaFtasse nau nCi ihsous.
mat 28:17 nterounau de eroF auouwSt naF Hoine de audisdaze.
mat 28:18 aFTpeFouoi eroou nCi ihsous aFSaJe nmmau eFJw mmos Je auT nai nexousia nim Hn tpe. auw HiJm pkaH.
mat 28:19 bwk Ce ntetnTsbw nnHeqnos throu. ntetnbaptize mmoou epran mpeiwt mn pShre mn pepneuma etouaab.
mat 28:20 etetnTsbw nau eHareH eHwb nim ntaiHonou etethutn. auw eis Hhhte anok TSoop nmmhtn nneHoou throu SaeHrai etsunteleia mpaiwn.
mar 1:1 = tarch mpeuaggelion nihsous pecristos [pShre mpnoute].
mar 1:2 kata petshH Hn hsaias peprofhths Je eis Hhhte TnaJeupaaggelos HiHh mmok nFsbte tekHih.
mar 1:3 peHroou mpetwS ebol Hn terhmos Je soutn teHih mpJoeis ntetn soutnneFmoit.
mar 1:4 aFSwpe de nCi iwHannhs eFTbaptisma mpJaie eFkhrusse noubaptisma mmetanoia epkw ebol nnnobe.
mar 1:5 auw asbwk naF ebol nCi tecwra thrs nToudaia nmna qierosoluma throu auJi baptisma ntootF Hm piordanhs piero euexomologi nneunobe.
mar 1:6 auw iwHannhs nereHenFw nCamoul to HiwwF ereoumoJ nSaar mhr eteFTpe. eFouemSJe Hiebiw nHoout.
mar 1:7 auw neFtaSeoiS eFJw mmos Je Fnhu mnnswei nCi petJoor eroei eangouHikanos an epaHt ebwl ebol mpmous mpeFtooue.
mar 1:8 anok aeiTbaptisma nhtn Hn oumoou. ntoF de eFnabaptize mmwtn Hn oupneuma eFouaab.
mar 1:9 = auw asSwpe Hn neHoou etmmau aFei nCi ihsous ebol Hn nazareq ntetgalilaia auw aFJibaptisma Hm piordanhs ntniwHannhs
mar 1:10 nteunou de eFnhu eHrai mpmoou aFnau emphue eauouwn auw pepneuma eFnhu epesht eJwF nqe nouCroompe
mar 1:11 auw ousmh asSwpe ebol Hn mphue Je ntok pe paShre pamerit entapaouwS Swpe nHhtk
mar 1:12 = auw teunou pepneuma aFJitF ebol eterhmos
mar 1:13 auw neFHnterhmos nHme nHoou erepsatanas peiraze mmoF eFSoop mn neqhrion. auw naggelos neudiakoni naF.
mar 1:14 = mnnsanseparadidou niwHannhs aFei nCi ihsous etgalilaia eFkhrusse mpeuaggelion mpnoute
mar 1:15 Je apeuoiS Jwk ebol auw asHwn eHoun nCi tmntrro mpnoute metanoi ntetnpisteue Hm peuaggelion.
mar 1:16 = auw eFmooSe Hatnteqalassa ntgalilaia aFnau esimwn nmandreas pson nsimwn eunouJSne eteqalassa neHenouwHe gar ne.
mar 1:17 peJaF nau nCi ihsous Je amhein oueHthutn nswei auw Tnarthutn nouwHe nreFCeprwme.
mar 1:18 nteunou de aukaneuSnhu auouaHou nswF
mar 1:19 auw ntereFmooSe eqh noukouei aFnau eiakwbos pShre nzebedaios nmiwHannhs peFson ntoou Hwou euHmpJoei eusobte nneuSnhu
mar 1:20 nteunou aFmoute eroou auw aukapeuiwt zebedaios Hm pJoei mnnJaibeke aubwk auouaHou nswF
mar 1:21 = aubwk de eHoun ekafarnaoum auw nteunou Hn nsabbaton aFTsbw Hn tsunagwgh
mar 1:22 auw aurSphre eJn teFsbw eFTsbw gar nau nqe an etouTsbw nCi negrammateus HwseuntFtexousia mmau
mar 1:23 auw nteunou neunourwme Hn tsunagwgh ere oupneuma nakaqarton nmmaF auw aFJiSkak ebol
mar 1:24 eFJw mmos Je aHrok nmman ihsous pnazwraios ntakei etakon Tsooun mmok Je ntknim ntkpetouaab mpnoute.
mar 1:25 auw ihsous aFepitima naF eFJw mmos Je tmrwk ngei ebol mmoF
mar 1:26 auw nterepepneuma nakaqarton raHtF epkaH auw aFwS ebol Hn ounoC nHroou aFei ebol mmoF
mar 1:27 auw aurHote throu Hwste nseSaJe nm neuerhu euJw mmos Je ou pe pai eisousbw bbrre Hn ouexousia nkepneuma nakaqarton FoueHsaHne nau auw seswtm nswF
mar 1:28 apeFsoeit bwk ebol nteunou Hm ma nim mpkwte thrF ntgalilaia.
mar 1:29 = nteunou de nterouei ebol Hn tsunagwgh aFbwk eHoun ephei nsimwn mnandreas nmiakwbos nmiwHannhs
mar 1:30 tSwme de nsimwn nesnhJ esHhm. auw nteunou auSaJe nmmaF etbhhts.
mar 1:31 aFTpeFouoei de eros aFtounos eaFamaHte ntesCiJ auw peHmom aFlo Hiwws asdiakoni nau.
mar 1:32 rouHe de ntereFSwpe pe ereprh naHwtp aueine naF nnetmokH throu mn neterendaimwnion nmmau
mar 1:33 auw tpolis thrs asswouH Hirmpro mphi.
mar 1:34 aFqerapou noumhhSe eumokH nSwne euSobe auw oumhhSe ndaimwnion aFnoJou ebol emaFkandaimwnion eSaJe ebol Je eusooun mmoF
mar 1:35 = auw Htoou emate ntereFtwoun aFbwk ebol euma nJaie aFSlhl mpnau etmmau
mar 1:36 auw aupwt ebol nswF nCi simwn mn netnmmaF autaHoF
mar 1:37 auw peJau naF Je sekwte nswk throu
mar 1:38 peJaF nau Je maron ekema enketmmo etHhn eHoun Jekaas eiekhrusse on nHhtou ntaiei gar ebol epeiHwb.
mar 1:39 auw aFbwk eFkhrusse Hn neusunagwgh Hn tgalilaia thrs auw nkedaimwnion eFnouJe mmoou ebol
mar 1:40 = auw aFei SaroF nCi ourwme eFsobH eFparakalei mmoF eFJw mmos naF Je ekSanouwS knatbboei
mar 1:41 auw ntereFSnHthF aFsoutntootF ebol auw aFkwH eroF eFJw mmos naF Je TouwS tbbo.
mar 1:42 auw nteunou apeFswbaH lo HiwwF aFtbbo.
mar 1:43 auw ntereFHwn etootF nteunou aFJoouF ebol
mar 1:44 eFJw mmos naF Je CwSt mprJoos nlaau. alla bwk ngtsabok epouhhb ngJi eHrai etbe pektbbo nnentamwushs oueHsaHne mmoou eumntmntre nau.
mar 1:45 ntereFei de ebol aFarcesqai ntaSeoiS nHaH auw esrpSaJe Hwste nFtmCmCom ebwk eHoun etpolis nouwnH alla neFHnHenma nJaie auw neunhu eratF ebol Hm ma nim.
mar 2:1 = ntereFbwk de eHoun ekafarnaoum HiJn HenHoou auswtm Je FHnouhei
mar 2:2 auw aumhhSe swouH emau Hwste ntetnmeS Hirmpro Sopou. auw aFSaJe nmmau Hm pSaJe.
mar 2:3 aueine de eratF nourwme eFshC ereFtoou nrwme Fi HaroF
mar 2:4 auw mpouSbwk naF eHoun etbe pmhhSe auCelptoueHsoi ebol mpma etFnHhtF auw nterouSoJt aucala mpeCloC epesht petere petshC nhJ HiJwF.
mar 2:5 auw ihsous ntereFnau eteupistis peJaF mpetshC Je paShre senakaneknobe nak ebol.
mar 2:6 neunHoine de nnegrammateus Hmoos mpma etmmau eumokmek Hn neuHht
mar 2:7 Je etbeou pai FSaJe Hinai eFJioua nim petnaSkanobe ebol nsapnoute maouaaF.
mar 2:8 auw nteunou ntereFeime Hm peFpneuma Je semokmek Hrai nHhtou peJaF nau Je etbeou tetnmeue enai Hn netnHht
mar 2:9 aS gar petmotn eJoos mpetshC Je twoun ngFipekCloC ngmooSe JneJoos Je senakaneknobe nak ebol
mar 2:10 Jekaas de etetnenau Je ountFexousia mmau nCi pShre mprwme ekanobe ebol HiJmpkaH peJaF mpetshC
mar 2:11 Je twoun eiJerok Fi mpekCloC bwk epekhei
mar 2:12 auw aFtwoun nteunou aFtalepeFCloC eJwF aFei ebol Hi qh mmoou throu Hwste nserSphre throu nseTeoou mpnoute euJw mmos Je mpnnau eouon eneH Hinai.
mar 2:13 = aFei on ebol Hatnqalassa auw pmhhSe thrF auswouH eroF aFTsbw nau
mar 2:14 auw eFparage aFnau eleouei pShre nalfaios eFHmoos HipeFtelwnion peJaF naF Je ouaHk nswei auw aFtwoun aFouaHF nswF.
mar 2:15 asSwpe de eFnhJ Hm peFhei aHaH ntelwnhs HireFrnobe noJou nmihsous mn neFmaqhths neuoS gar. auw auaHou nswF
mar 2:16 negrammateus mn nefarissaios nterounau Je Fouwm nmnreFrnobe auw ntelwnhs peJau nneFmaqhths Je etbeou Fouwm auw Fsw nmnreFrnobe auw ntelwnhs
mar 2:17 auw ihsous ntereFswtm peJaF nau Je nsercria an nCi netthk mpsain alla netSoop kakws ntaei an eteHmndikaios alla rreFrnobe.
mar 2:18 = auw mmaqhths niwHannhs nmna nefarissaios neunhsteue. auei de naF euJw mmos Je etbeou mmaqhths niwHannhs auw mmaqhths nnefarissaios senhsteue nekmaqhths de nsenhsteue an
mar 2:19 peJe ihsous nau Je mh ounCom etreunhsteue nCi nShre mpma nSeleet Hoson erepatSeleet nmmau. Hoson patSeleet nmmau nsenaSnhsteue an.
mar 2:20 ounHenHoou de nhu Hotan euSanFi ntootou mpatSeleet tote senanh steue Hn neHoou etmmau
mar 2:21 - merelaau neJtoeis nSaei ernSthn mplCe eSwpe mmon ttoeis nSai naFipkwte mmau nteSthn mplCe nspwH nHouo.
mar 2:22 auw merelaau neJhrp bbrre eHwt nas eSwpe mmon phrp napeHnHwt ntephrp pwn ebol ntenHwt tako. alla eSauneJhrp bbrre eHwt bbrre.
mar 2:23 = auw asSwpe Hn nsabbaton etreFmooSe ebol Hn niwHe etrht auw neFmaqhths eumooSe auarcitlk Hms.
mar 2:24 nefarrisaios de peJau naF Je anau Je eurou Hn nsabbaton eouk exesti eaaF.
mar 2:25 peJaF nau Je mpetnoSF laau Je ntadaueid rou ntereFHko ntoF mn netnmmaF
mar 2:26 Je naS nHe aFbwk eHoun ephi mpnoute Hiabiaqar parciereus auw noik nteproqesis aFouomou eouk exesti naF eouomou nsanouhhb auw aFT nnkooue etnmmaF.
mar 2:27 peJaF on nau Je psabbaton ntaFSwpe etbe prwme. auw ntaprwme Swpe an etbe psabbaton.
mar 2:28 Hwste pShre mprwme pJoeis pe mpkesabbaton.
mar 3:1 = auw aFbwk on eHoun etsunagwgh neunourwme de mmau ereteFCiJ moout
mar 3:2 auw neuparathri eroF Je eneFnaqerapou mmoF Hn nsabbaton Je euekathgori mmoF
mar 3:3 auw peJaF mprwme ereteFCiJ moout Je twoung amou etmhte.
mar 3:4 auw peJaF nau Je exesti Hn nsabbaton erpetnanouF Jnrpeqoou etanHeouyuch Jnemoouts. ntoou de aukarwou
mar 3:5 auw ntereFCwSt eHoun eHrau Hn ouorgh eFmokH nHht eJmptwm nHht mpeuHht peJaF mprwme Je soutntekCiJ ebol aFsoutwns auw aslo nCi teFCiJ.
mar 3:6 nterouei de ebol nteunou nCi nefarissaios nmnHhrwdianos auJiSoJne eroF Jekaas euetakoF
mar 3:7 = auw ihsous aFanacwri mn neFmaqhths ebol eteqalassa. auw ounoC mmhhSe ebol Hn tgalilaia auouaHou nswF nmToudaia
mar 3:8 nmqierosoluma auw kenoC mmhhSe ebol Hn Tdoumaia mn pekro mpiordanhs nmpkwte nturos nmsidwn euswtm enetFeire mmoou auei SaroF
mar 3:9 auw aFJoos nneFmaqhths Je ereHeneJhu proskarteri eroF etbe pmhhSe Je neuqlibe mmoF
mar 3:10 naSe nentaFtalCoou gar Hwste etreuTpeuoi eroF Je eueJwH eroF. auw netemmastigx Hiwou

mar 3:12 auw neFepitima nau emate Je nneuouonHF ebol.
mar 3:13 = aFbwk de eHrai eptoou auw aFmoute enetFouaSou
mar 3:14 aFneHmntsnoous ebol [nHhtou nai ntaFT pinou neapostolos] Je eueSwpe nmmaF auw nFJoouse ebol etaSeoiS
mar 3:15 nFT nau ntexousia eneJ daimwnion ebol
mar 3:16 auw aFtaHo eratou mpmntsnoous auw simwn aFTouran eroF Je petros.
mar 3:17 auw iakwbos pShre nzebedaios nmiwHanhs pson niakwbos. aFTHenran eroou Je boanhrges ete pai pe nShre mpeHroubbaei.
mar 3:18 auw andreas nmfilippos nmbarqolomaios. mnmaqaios. nmqwmas auw iakwbos pShre nalfaios mnqaddaios auw simwn pkananaios
mar 3:19 nmioudas piskariwths pentaFparadidou mmoF
mar 3:20 = auw aFei eHoun ephei apmhhSe on swouH eroF Hwste nsetmsrFe eouempeuoeik
mar 3:21 nterouswtm de nCi neFrwme auei ebol eamaHte mmoF neuJw gar mmos Je apeFHht pwSs.
mar 3:22 auw negrammateus ntauei ebol Hn qierosoluma neuJw mmos Je erebeelzeboul nmmaF auw Hm parcwn nndaimwnion eFneJdaimwnion ebol
mar 3:23 aFmoute de eroou aFSaJe nmmau Hn Henparabolh eFJw mmos Je naS nHe psatanas FnaneJpsatanas ebol
mar 3:24 auw erSanoumntrro pwrJ eneserhunsnaSaHe an erats nCi tmntrro etmmau.
mar 3:25 auw erSanouhei pwrJ eneFerhu nneSphei etmmau aHeratF.
mar 3:26 auw eSJe psatanas aFtwoun ntoF eJwF auw aFpwrJ nneFeSaHeratF. alla ateFHah Swpe.
mar 3:27 alla mnlaau naSbwk eHoun ephei mpJwwre nFtwrp nneFHnaou eFtmmour nSorp mpJwwr. auw tote nFtwrp mpeFhei.
mar 3:28 Hamhn TJw mmos nhtn Je nobe nim Hioua nim etounaJoou nCi nShre nrrwme senakaau nau ebol
mar 3:29 petnaJioua de epepneuma etouaab mmntFkw ebol Sa eneH alla FChp eunobe Sa eneH.
mar 3:30 ebol Je seJw mmos Jeoupneuma nakaqarton nmmaF.
mar 3:31 = auw auei nCi teFmaau mn neFsnhuauaHeratou Hibol auw auJoou naF eHoun eumoute eroF

mar 3:33 aFouwSb de eFJw mmos nau Je nim te tamaau auw nim ne nasnhu

mar 4:1 = aFarcesqai on eTsbw Hateqalassa. auw aunoC mmhhSe swouH eroF Hwste etreFale epJoei nFHmoos Hn teqalassa. auw pmhhSe thrF neFaHeratF Hipekro nqalassa
mar 4:2 aFTsbw de nau emate Hn Henparabolh auw neFJw mmos nau Hn teFsbw
mar 4:3 Je swtm eis Hhhte aFei ebol nCi petJo etJo.
mar 4:4 auw ntereFJo oua men aFHe HateteHih auw auei nCi nHalate auomou
mar 4:5 keua de aFHe eHrai eJn tpetra pma etemmnHaH nkaH nHhtF auw nteunou auTouw eHraei etbe JemnHaH nkaH Haroou
mar 4:6 auw ntereprh Sa auHwCb auw etbe JempouJenoune ebol auSooue
mar 4:7 keua aFHe eHraei eJn nSonte auw auei eHraei nCi nSonte auoCtou auw mpouTkarpos
mar 4:8 Henkooue auHe eJmpkaH etnanouF auw auei eHrai auauxane auTkarpos emaab auw ese auw eSe.
mar 4:9 neFJw de mmos nau Je peteuntFmaaJe mmau eswtm mareFswtm.
mar 4:10 = ntereFka pmhhSe de auJnouF nCi netnmmaF nmpmntsnoous enparabolh
mar 4:11 peJaF nau. Je ntwtn ntauT nhtn mpmusthrion ntmntrro mpnoute nh de etHibol eunaJiHwb nim eroou Hn Henparabolh
mar 4:12 Jekaas eunau euenau auw nsetmnau auw euswtm eueswtm nsetmnoei. mhpws nsekotou nsekw nau ebol.
mar 4:13 = auw peJaF nau Je ntetnsooun an nteiparabolh. auw pws nkeparabolh throu tetnasouwnou
mar 4:14 petJo eFJo mpSaJe.
mar 4:15 nai de ne etHateteHih mpma eSauJepSaJe nHhtF. auw eSauswtm nteunou SaFei nCi psatanas nFFipSaJe entauJoF nHhtou
mar 4:16 auw nai Hwou nentauJoou HiJn mma mpetra eSauswtm epSaJe nteunou SauJitF Hn ouraSe
mar 4:17 mmnnoune de Hrai nHhtou alla Hn prosouoeiS ne erSanouqliyis de Swpe houdiwgmos etbe pSaJe nteunou Sauskandalize.
mar 4:18 auw Henkooue nentauJoou eHrai enSonte etenai ne ntauswtm epSaJe
mar 4:19 auw proouS mpaiwn nmtapath ntmntrmmao auw nkeepiqumia etbhk eHoun eroou sewCt mpSaJe auw nFTkarpos an ebol
mar 4:20 auw nh ne ntauJoou eJmpkaH etnanouF euswtm epSaJe seSwp mmoF eroou auw setauekarpos ebol Hn maab auw Hn se auw Hn Se.
mar 4:21 = peJaF de nau Je mh erepHhbs naei Je euekaaF HaouSi. hHaouCloC mh neunakaaF an HiJn tlucnia.
mar 4:22 mmnpetHobs gar ensenaColpF an ebol. oude mmnpetHhp enFnaouwnH an ebol.
mar 4:23 peteuntFmaaJe mmau eswtm mareFswtm
mar 4:24 - auw neFJw mmos Je THthtn Je ou petetnswtm eroF. Hm pSi etetnaSi mmoF senaSi nhtn nHhtF.
mar 4:25 peteuntaF gar senaT naF. auw petemntaF auw peteuntaFsF senaFitF ntootF.
mar 4:26 = neFJw de mmos nau Je tai te qe ntmntrro mpnoute eso nqe nourwme eFSannouJe mpeFCroC eHrai epeFkaH.
mar 4:27 auw nFnkotk nFtwoun nteuSh mn peHoou SarepeCroC Touw nFrnoC enFsooun an
mar 4:28 ntoF nqe pkaH SaFTouw eHraei mauaaF Sorp men noucortos mnnswF ouHms auw ousouo eFmeH Hm pHms
mar 4:29 erSanpkarpos de pwH nteunou SaFnpoHs Je apte mpwHs Swpe
mar 4:30 = auw neFJw mmos Je einatntn tmntrro mpnoute eou. hennakaas eHrai Hn aS mparabolh
mar 4:31 ennakaas nqe noublbile nSltm euSanJos eHrai epkaH essobk men eneCrwC throu etHiJmpkaH
mar 4:32 auw euSanJos Sasei eHrai nsJise enouoote throu nstauo ebol nHennoC nklados Hwste nseSouwH HatesHaeibes nCi nHalate ntpe
mar 4:33 = auw Hn naismot mparabolh throu neFJw eroou mpSaJe kataqe etounaSswtm
mar 4:34 aJnparabolh de meFSaJe nmmau nsausa de SaFbolou throu eneFmaqhths.
mar 4:35 = auw peJaF nau Hm peHoou etmmau ntererouHe Swpe Je maron epikro
mar 4:36 aukapmhhSe Ce autaloF epJoei nqe etFnHhts aHenkeeJhu sChr nmmaF.
mar 4:37 auw aunoC nHathu Swpe anHoeim FwCe epJoei Hwste eomsF.
mar 4:38 ntoF de neFHipaHou mpJoei eFnkotk HiJn ouSot auw auneHse mmoF euJw mmos naF. Je psaH ngo an pe rroouS Je tnnamou
mar 4:39 aFtwounF de aFepitima mpthu auw peJaF nteqalassa Je karw nteStmrw auw apthu HrhC aunoC nJamh Swpe.
mar 4:40 auw peJaF nau Je aHrwtn tetno nCabHht mpatetnkapistis nhtn.
mar 4:41 auw aurHote Hn ounoC nHote euJw mmos nneuerhu Je ouaS mmine pe pai Je pkethu nmteqalassa swtm nswF.

act 26:3 malista eksooun nnswnt throu. auw nzhthma nnioudai. etbe pai Tsops mmok eswtm eroi Hn oumntHarSHht.

act 26:8 etbe ou Fo napistos nnaHrhtn. eSJe pnoute natounes netmoout.
act 26:9 anok Ce neaikaas Ha iat pe eT oube pran nihsous pecristos pnazwraios epeHouo.
act 26:10 pai Ce aiaaF Hn qierosoluma eaineJ HaH nnetouaab epeSteko. eaiJi texousia ebol Hitn narciereus. auw on aiTpzhfos etakoou.
act 26:11 neidimwri de mmoou nHaH nsop Hn sunagwgh nim eianagkaze mmoou eJioua epeFran auw eiCont eroou epeHouo neidiwke nswou SaHrai empolis etouhu.
act 26:12 = einabwk de edamaskos Hn texousia ntaiJits ntnnarciereus.
act 26:13 anau eprro Hn teHih mpnou mmeere euouoein eaFpira ebol Hn tpe eHoue pouoein mprh aFSa eHrai eJwi mn netmooSe nmmai.
act 26:14 auw nternHe thrn eHrai eJm pkaH ebol Hn qote aiswtm eusmh esJw mmos nai ntaspe mmntHebraios Je saule saule aHrok kpht nswi smokH nak eTtbhr eHoun Hn Hensoure.
act 26:15 anok de peJai Je ntk nim pJoeis. peJe pJoeis nai Je anok pe ihsous petkpht nswF.
act 26:16 alla twoun ngaHeratk HiJn nekouerhte etbe pai gar aiouwnH nak ebol etoSk nHuphreths auw mmntre nqe ntaknau eroi auw nqe eTnaouwnH nak ebol

act 26:18 eouwn nneubal ektoou ebol Hm pkake epouoein auw ebol Hn texousia mpsatanas eHoun epnoute etreuJi mpkw ebol nneunobe auw ouklhros mn netouaab Hm ptreupisteue eroi.
act 26:19 = etbe pai Ce prro agrippa mpiratswtm epCwlp ebol ntaFSwpe nai ebol Hn tpe.
act 26:20 alla aikhrusse nSorp Hn damaskos auw Hn qierosoluma mn tecwra thrs nnioudai mn nHeqnos etreumetanoi auw nsektoou epnoute eueire nneHbhue eumpSa ntmetanoia.
act 26:21 etbe pai Ce nioudai auCopt Hm perpe auHitootou eHotbet.
act 26:22 aimate de noubohqia ebol Hitm pnoute eiaHerat SaHrai epoou nHoou. eirmntre nnkoui mn nnoC. nTJe laau an pbol nnenta neprofhths mn mwushs Joou eunaSwpe
act 26:23 Je pecristos naSopou. auw pSorp pe ntwoun ebol Hn netmoout. auw FnaJw nouoein mplaos mn nHeqnos.
act 26:24 = nai de eFtauo mmoou peJe fhstos naF Hn ounoC nsmh Je paule klobe. apeHoue sHai lebtk.
act 26:25 paulos de peJaF Je nTlobe an fhste pekratistos. alla eiJw nHenSaJe mme Hi mntrmnHht.

1th 1:1 = paulos mn silouanos mn timoqeos eusHai ntekklhsia nneqessalonikeus Hm pnoute peneiwt mn pJoeis ihsous pecristos. tecaris nhtn mn Trhnh.

rev 6:13 nsiou ntpe auHe eHrai eJm pkaH nqe noubw nknte esnouJe ebol nnesCwwbe ereounoC nthu kim eros
rev 6:14 tpe asCwl nqe nouJwwme eFChl toou nim Hinhsos nim aukim ebol Hn neuma.
rev 6:15 auw nrrwou mpkaH mn nnoC mn nciliarcos mn nrmmao mn nJwwre auw HmHal nim HirmHe auHopou Hn nespulaion mn nsibt nentoueih euJw mmos

rev 6:17 Je aFei nCi pnoC nHoou nteForgh nim petnaSaHeratF.
rev 7:1 = mnnsa nai anau eFtoou naggelos euaHeratou epeFtoou nkooH mpkaH euamaHte mpeFtoou nthu mpkaH Je nnethu niFe eJm pkaH heJn qallassa heJn laau nShn.
rev 7:2 auw anau ekeaggelos eFnhu ebol Hn mma nSa mprh eoun ousfragis ntootF nte pnoute etonH aFJi Skak ebol Hn ounoC nsmh epeFtoou naggelos nentautaas nau etake pkaH mn qallassa
rev 7:3 eFJw mmos Je mprtake pkaH mn qallassa mn nShn Santntwwbe nenHmHal mpennoute eHrai eJn teuteHne.
rev 7:4 auw aiswtm ethpe nnentausfragize mmoou mn taFte ntba mn Ftoou nSo ebol Hn fulh nim nenShre mpeisrahl
rev 7:5 ebol Hn tefulh niouda mn tsnoous nSo eutoobe ebol Hn tefulh nHroubhn mn tsnoous nSo ebol Hn tefulh ngad mn tsnoous nSo
rev 7:6 ebol Hn tefulh nashr mn tsnoous nSo ebol Hn tefulh nefqaleim mn tsnoous nSo ebol Hn tefulh mmanassh mn tsnoous nSo

rev 7:8 ebol Hn tefulh nzaboulon mn tsnoous nSo ebol Hn tefulh niwshf mn tsnoous nSo ebol Hn tefulh nbeniamin mn tsnoous nSo eutoobe.
rev 7:9 = mnnsa nai de anau auw eisounoC mmhhSe enaSwF emn laau naeSC mCom eopF ebol Hn Heqnos nim Hi fulh Hiaspe euaHeratou mpmto ebol mpeqronos mn pmto ebol mpeHieib euCoole nHenstolh nouwbS ereHenba Hn neuCiJ
rev 7:10 euaSkak ebol Hn ounoC nsmh euJw mmos Je pouJai mpennoute etHmoos Hi peqronos mn peHieib.
rev 7:11 auw naggelos throu neuaHeratou mpkwte mpeqronos mn nepresbuteros mn peFtoou nzwon auw aupaHtou eJm peuHo mpmto ebol mpeqronos auouwSt mpnoute euJw mmos
rev 7:12 Je Hamhn pesmou mn peoou mn tsofia auw teucaristeia mn ptaio mn tCom mn pamaHte mpennoute Sa eneH neneH Hamhn.
rev 7:13 - aFouwSb nCi oua ebol Hn nepresbeteros eFJw mmos nai Je nim ne nai etCoole nneistolh nouwbS auw ntauei ebol twn.
rev 7:14 peJai naF Je pJoeis ntok etsooun peJaF nai Je nai ne netnhu ebol Hn tnoC nqliyis eaueiw nneustolh autbboou mpesnoF mpeHieib.
rev 7:15 etbe pai sempmto ebol mpeqronos mpnoute euSmSe naF mpeHoou mn teuSh Hm peFrpe auw petHmoos Hi peFqronos FnarHaibes eroou. nsenaHko an

rev 8:1 = ntereFouwn ntmeHsaSFe nsfragis aukarwou Hrai Hn tpe naouCis ounou.

rev 8:3 - auw aFei nCi keaggelos aFaHeratF eJm pequsiasthrion eoun ouSourh nnoub ntootF auT naF nHenSouHhne enaSwou Jekaas eFeT eHrai mn neSlhl nnetouaab throu eJm pequsiasthrion nnoub etmpmto ebol mpeqronos.

rev 8:7 - pSorp naggelos aFsalpize auw aFSwpe nCi oualmpe mn oukwHt euthH mn ousnoF aunoJF eHrai eJm pkaH auw pou nSomnt mpkaH aFrwkH.
rev 8:8 - aFsalpize nCi pmeHsnau naggelos auw nqe nounoC ntoou eFJero Hn oukwHt aunoJF eHrai eJn qallassa auw pounSomnt nqallassa aFrsnoF
rev 8:9 auw aumou nCi pou nSomnt nenswnt nqallassa ete oun yuch nHhtou auw pou nSomnt nneJhu aFtako.
rev 8:10 - pmeHSomnt naggelos aFsalpize auw aFHe ebol Hn tpe nCi ounoC nsiou eFJero nqe noulampas aFei eHrai eJm pounSomnt nneierwou mn npugh nmmoou

rev 8:12 - pmeHFtoou naggelos aFsalpize auw pou nSomnt mprh aFSwwCe mn pounSomnt mpooH mn pou nSomnt nensiou Jekaas eFerkake nCi pounSomnt auw peHoou neFtmrouoein mpeFounSomnt mn teuSh on ntHe.
rev 8:13 - anau auw aiswtm euaitos eFHhl Hn tmhhte ntpe eFJw mmos Hn ounoC nsmh Je ouoi nSomnt nsop ouoi nnetouhhH HiJm pkaH ebol Hm pkeseph nHroou naggelos nai etnasalpize.
rev 9:1 = pmeHTou naggelos aFsalpize auw anau eusiou aFHe ebol Hn tpe eHrai eJm pkaH auw auT naF mpSoSt ntSwte mpnoun

rev 9:3 auw aHenSJe ei eHrai eJm pkaH auT nau nouexousia nqe ete ountau exousia mmau nCi nouwHe mpkaH.
rev 9:4 auJoos nau Jekaas nneutake pecortos mpkaH auw Shn nim ei mhti nrwme ete mntau mmau ntesfragis mpnoute eJn teuteHne.

rev 9:8 eun HenFw HiJwou nqe mpFw nneHioome ere neuobHe onqe nnaneimoui
rev 9:9 eun HenHwk Hiwou nqe nHenHwk mpenipe ere peHroou nneutnH onqe mpeHroou nHenHarma mn HenHtwwr enaSwou eupht eppolemos

rev 9:12 - eis ouoi aFouei ne eis Hhhte senhu nCi keouoi snau.

rev 9:15 auw aubwl mpeFtoou naggelos nai etsbtwt eteunou mn peHoou mn pebot mn terompe Jekaas euemoout mpounSomnt nenrwme.
rev 9:16 auw thpe nnestrateuma nneHtwwr pe tba ntba nsep snau aiswtm eteuhpe.
rev 9:17 auw tai ta qe ntainau epeine nneHtwwr mn netale eroou eun HenHwk Hiwou nauan nkwHt Hi Huakinqinon Hi qhn ere napeue nneHtwwr o nqe nnaphue nmmoui eFnhu ebol Hn rwou nCi oukwHt mnoukapnos mnouqhn.

rev 9:21 oude mpoume tanoi ebol Hn neuHwtb mn neuHik mn neuporneia.
rev 10:1 = anau ekeaggelos eFCmCom eFnhu ebol Hn tpe ere oukloole HiwF ere ouoein HiJn teFaph ere peFHo onqe mprh ere neFourhhte o nqe nHenstulos nkwHt

rev 10:3 aFaSkak ebol Hn ounoC nsmh nqe noumoui eFlHhm ntereFaSkak de ebol auSaJe nCi tsaSFe nHroubbai Hn neuaspe.
rev 10:4 auw nterouSaJe nCi tsaSFe nHroubbai Hn neuaspe. aiei de einaseH ne ntauJoou nCi tsaSFe nHroubbai aiswtm eusmh ebol Hn tpe esJw mmos Je twwbe ernnentauJoou nCi neHroubbai ngtmsaHou.

rev 10:9 aibwk Sa paggelos peJaF nai Je ma nai mpJwwme peJaF nai Je JitF ngouomF auw FnaSwpe eFsaSe nHhtk alla FnaHloC Hn tektapro nqe nouebiw..

rev 11:1 = auw auT nai noukaS eFeine nouCerwb euJw mmos Je twoun ngSi prpe mpnoute mn pequsiasthrion mn netouwSt Hrai nHhtF.

rev 11:10 auw netouhhH HiJm pkaH senaraSe mmoou nseounoF nseJoou nHehdwron nneuerhu Je piprofuths snau aubasanize nnetouhhH HiJm pkaH.

rev 12:4 auw peFsat aFswk mpou nSomnt nensiou ntpe aFnoJou eHrai eJm pkaH auw pedrakwn aFaHeratF mpmto ebol ntesHime tai etnamise Jekaas esSanJpepesShre eFeouomF.

rev 12:10 aiswtm eunoC nsmh ebol Hn tpe esJw mmos Je tenou aFSwpe nCi pouJai mn tCom auw tmntrro mpennoute auw texousia mpeFcristos Je aunouJ epesht mpkathgoros nnensnhu petkathgorei mmoou mpmto ebol mpnoute mpeHoou mn teuSh.

rev 12:12 etbe pai eufrane mphue mn netouhhH nHhtou. ouoi mpkaH mn qallassa Je apdiabolos ei epesht Sarwtn mn ounoC nCwnt eFsooun Je kekoui nouoeiS pete ountaF sF.
rev 12:13 - ntereFnau de nCi pedrakwn Je aunoJF epesht eJm pkaH aFpwt nsa tesHime ntasJpe pSr Hoout.
rev 12:14 auw auT ntesHime ntnH snau naeitos Jekaas eseHwl ebol eterhmos epesma etounasanouSs nHhtF nouoeiS mn HenouoeiS mn tpaSe nouoeiS mpmto ebol mpHoF.

rev 13:1 = anau euqurion eFnhu eHrai Hn qallassa eunmht ntap mmoF auw saSFe nape ere mhte nCrhpe HiJn neFaphue eFshH eJn neFaphue nCi ouran nJioua.

rev 13:3 auw ouei ebol Hn neFaphue eSJe ntauHotbes epmou. auw teplugh mpeFmou autalCos apkaH thrF rSphre HipaHou mpequrion
rev 13:4 auw auouwSt mpedrakwn Je aFT ntexousia mpequrion auw auouwSt mpequrion euJw mmos Je nim pettntwn eroF hnim pete ounCom mmoF emiSe nmmaF.

rev 13:9 - pete ountF maaJe mareFswtm.
rev 13:10 petaicmalwtize senaFitF etaic malwsia petnaHwtb Hn oushFe senaHotbeF Hn tshFe. pai pe pma ntHupomonh mn tpisTs nnetouaab.

rev 13:12 eFeire ntexousia thrs mpequrion nSorp mpeFmto ebol auw aFtre pkaH mn netouhhH nHhtF ouwSt mpequrion nSorp pai ntautalCe teplugh mpeFmou.
rev 13:13 auw Fnaeire nHennoC mmaein Hws de nFtre pkwHt ei ebol Hn tpe eJm pkaH mpmto ebol nenrwme
rev 13:14 nFplana nnetouhhH HiJm pkaH etbe mmaein ntautaau naF eaau mpmto ebol mpequrion eFJw mmos nnetouhhH Hrai HiJm pkaH Je tamio nouHikwn mpequrion etereteplugh ntshFe HiwwF auw aFwnH.
rev 13:15 auw auT naF etreFT pneuma nqikwn mpequrion Jekaas eseSaJe nCi qikwn mpequrion auw Fnasmnts Jekaas netensenaouwSt an mpequrion euemooutou.
rev 13:16 auw Fnataas nouon nim nkoui mn nnoC nrmmao mn nHhke nrmHe mn nHmHal Jekaas eueT nau nHensHai eJn teuCiJ nounam heJn teuteHne
rev 13:17 Je nne laau SCmCom eSwp heT ebol eimhti pete ountaF pesHai mpequrion hpeFran.
rev 13:18 pai pe pma ntsofia pete oun Hht mmoF mareFep thpe mpran mpequrion thpe gar nourwme te eseire nseu Se seta se.
rev 14:1 = anau auw eis ouHieib eFaHeratF HiJm ptoou nsiwn auw mn taFte ntba mn Ftoou nSo eunmmaF euntau mmau mpeFran mn pran mpeFeiwt eFshH eHrai eJn teuteHne.
rev 14:2 auw aiswtm eusmh ebol Hn tpe nqe mpeHroou nHenmoou enaSwou auw nqe ntesmh nHennoC nHroubbai auw tesmh ntaiswtm eros eso nqe nHenCi qarodos euCiqarize nneukiqara.
rev 14:3 auw euJw nouJw nbrre mpmto ebol mpeqronos mn pmto ebol mpeFtoou nzwon mn nepresbeteros auw nemnSCom nlaau eeime etwdh ei mhti pmntaFte ntba mn peFtoou nSo nentauSoopou ebol Hm pkaH.
rev 14:4 nai ete mpoutwlm mn sHime eHenparqenos gar ne nai etmooSe mn peHieib epma eteFna eroF nai nentauSopou ebol Hn nrwme nouaparch mpnoute mn peHieib
rev 14:5 auw mpouHe eCol Hn teutapro Henatnobe gar ne.
rev 14:6 = anau euaggelos eFHhl Hn tmhhte ntpe eoun oueuaggelion ntootF nSa eneH etaSeoeiS nnetHmoos eHrai eJm pkaH auw eJn nHeqnos nim Hi fulh Hi aspe Hi laos
rev 14:7 eFJw mmos Hn ounoC nsmh Je ariHote HhtF mpnoute ntetn Teoou naF Je asei nCi teunou nteFkrisis auw ntetn ouwSt mpentaFtamietpe mn pkaH mn qallassa mn mpugh nmmoou.
rev 14:8 - akeaggelos mmeHsnau ouaHF nswF eFJw mmos Je asHe asHe nCi tnoC nbabulwn auw anHeqnos throu He Hm phrp mpCwnt ntesporneia.
rev 14:9 - akemeHSomnt naggelos ouaHF nswou eFJw mmos Hn ounoC nsmh Je petnaouwSt mpequrion hteFHikwn auw neFJi neFsHai eJn teFteHne.
rev 14:10 heJn teFCiJ. ntoF HwF on Fnasw ebol Hm phrp mpCwnt mpnoute pai etkura nagraton Hm pJw nteForgh auw senabasanize mmoou Hn oukwHt m nouqhn mpmto ebol nnaggelos etouaab mpmto ebol mpeHi eib.
rev 14:11 auw pkapnos nteubasanos naJi se eHrai Sa eneH neneH nsetmJimton mpeHoou mn teuSh nCi netnaouwSt mpequrion mn teFHikwn mn petnaJi mpmaein mpeFran.
rev 14:12 pai pe pma nqupomonh nnetouaab netHareH enentolh mpnoute mn tpistis nihsous.
rev 14:13 - aiswtm eusmh ebol Hn tpe esJw mmos Je sHai Je naiatou nnetnamou Jin ntenou Hm pJoeis se peJaF nCi pepneuma Jekaas euemton mmoou ebol Hn neuHise neuHbhue gar naouaHou nswou.
rev 14:14 = anau auw eis oukloole esouobS auw eFHmoos HiJn tekloole nCi peine nouShre nrwme eoun ouklom nnoub HiJn teFaph eunouoHs eFthm Hn teFCiJ.
rev 14:15 auw keaggelos aFei ebol Hm prpe eFaSkak ebol Hn ounoC nsmh eptHmoos eJn tekloole Je maJoou mpekoHs ngwHs Je asei nCi teunou mpwHs Je aFSooue nCi pwHs mpkaH.
rev 14:16 auw aFnouJ nCi petHmoos eJn tekloole mpeFoHs eHrai eJm pkaH auw aFwHs mpkaH.
rev 14:17 akeaggelos ei ebol Hm prpe etHn tmhte eun ouHalkou ntootF esthm.
rev 14:18 akeaggelos ei ebol Hm pequsiasturion euntaF texousia mpkwHt aFmoute Hn ounoC nsmh epetere qalkou ntootF esthm eFJw mmos Je maJoou mpekHalkou ngJwwle nnesmaH ntbw neloole mpkaH Je aupwH nCi neseloole.
rev 14:19 auw apaggelos nouJ nteFHalkou eHrai eJm pkaH aFJwwle ntbw neloole mpkaH auw aFnouJ eteHrwt noC mpCwnt mpnoute.
rev 14:20 auHwm nteHrwt pbol ntpolis auw apesnoF ei ebol Hn teHrwt Sa Hrai enecalinos nneHtwwr namntase nSe nstadion.
rev 15:1 = anau ekenoC mmaein nSphre Hn tpe saSF naggelos ere saSFe mplugh ntootou nHah Je Hrai nHhtou ntaFJwk ebol nCi pCwnt mpnoute.
rev 15:2 - anau nqe nouqallassa nabaChein esthH m noukwHt auw netnaJro ebol Hm pequrion mn teFHikwn mn thpe mpeFran neuaHeratou HiJn ouqallassa nabaChein ereHenkiqara ntootu ntepnoute.
rev 15:3 euJw ntwdh mmwushs pHmHal mpnoute mn twdh mpeHieib euJw mmos Je HennoC auw HenSphre ne nekHbhue pJoeis pnoute ppantwkratwr Hendikaiosunh auw Henme ne nekHbhue mn nekHiooue nnaiaiwn
rev 15:4 nim pete neFrHote Hhtk an pJoeis auw neFTeoou mpekran Je ntok mauaak pe petouaab auw pdikaios Je nHeqnos throu nhu nseouwSt mpekmto ebol Je anekdikaiwma ouwnH ebol.
rev 15:5 - mnnsa nai aFouwn nCi prpe nteskunh mpmntre ntpe
rev 15:6 auw auei ebol nCi psaSF naggelos etere tsaSFe mplugh ntootou ebol Hm prpe ere HenHbsw Hiwou euouobS eutbbhu eumhr eJn teumestnHht noumoJHF nnoub.
rev 15:7 auw oua ebol Hm peFtoou nzwon aFT mpsaSF naggelos nsaSFe mfialh nnoub eumeH ebol Hm pCwnt mpnoute etonH Sa nieneH neneH.

rev 16:1 = aiswtm eunoC nsmh ebol Hn tpe esJw mmos nnaggelos Je pwHt nnefialh mpCwnt mpnoute.
rev 16:2 - aFbwk nCi pSorp aFpwHt nteFfialh eHrai eJm pkaH auw aFSwpe nCi ousaS mponhron eFHoou eJn neteountau pmaein mpequrion mn netouwSt nteFHikwn.
rev 16:3 - apmeHsnau pwHt nteFfialh eHrai eJn qallassa asrsnoF nqe mpa netmoout auw aumou nCi yuch nim etonH Hn qallassa.
rev 16:4 - apmeHSomnt pwHt nteFfialh eJn neierwou mn npugh nmmoou auw aursnoF.

rev 16:6 Je aupwHt ebol mpesnoF nneprofhths auw akT nau nousnoF esooF Je sempSa.

rev 16:11 auw nuJioua pe epnoute ntpe ebol Hn neutkas mn neusaS auw mpoumetanoei ebol Hn neuHbhue.
rev 16:12 - apmeHsoou pwHt nteFfialh eJm peiero nnoC peufraths auw aFSooue nCi peFmoou Jekaas euesobte nteHih nneierwou ebol Hn mmanSa mprh.
rev 16:13 anau eunhu ebol Hn rwF mpedrakwn mn pequrion mn rwF mpeprofuths nnouJ nCi Somnt mpneuma nakaqarton nqe nHenkrour.
rev 16:14 Henpneuma gar ndaimwnion ne eueire nHenmaein etreueine ebol nnerrwou ntoikoumenh thrs esoouHou eHoun eppolemos mpnoC nHoou nte pnoute ppantwkratwr.
rev 16:15 eis Hhhte Tnhu nqe noureFJi oue naiatF mpetroeis auw etHareH eneFHoite Je nnFmooSe eFkh kaHhu nsenau epeFSipe.

rev 16:18 auSwpe nCi HenebrhCe mn Hensmh mn HenHroubbai mn ounoC nkmto ete mpe ouon nteFHe Swpe Jin ntauJp erwme HiJm pkaH ounoC nkmto nTCot.
rev 16:19 tnoC mpolis asrSomnt nouwn mn npolis nenHeqnos auHe auw tbabulwn nnoC aur pesmeeue mpmto ebol mpnoute eTnas mpJw mphrp mpCwnt nteForgh.

rev 16:21 ounoC nalampe eFnarouCis CinCwr nHrhSe aFHwou ebol Hn tpe eHrai eJn nrwme auw anrwme Jioua epnoute ebol Hn teplugh ntecalaza Je ounoC emate te tesplugh.
rev 17:1 = aFei nCi oua ebol Hm psaSF naggelos ete ountou tsaSFe mfialh aFSaJe nmmai eFJw mmos Je amou ntatsabok epHap ntnoC mpornh tetHmoos eHrai eJn Henmoou enaSwou
rev 17:2 tai ntauporneue nmmas nCi nrrwou mpkaH auw auTHe nCi netouhhH HiJm pkaH ebol Hm phrp ntesporneia
rev 17:3 aFJit Hm pepneuma ebol eterumos. auw anau eusHime estalhu euqurion nkokkos eFmeH nran noua eoun saSFe naph mmoF mn mht ntap.
rev 17:4 auw tesHime nesCoole nJhCe Hi kokkos Hi noub Hi enemme Hi margariths eun ouJw nnoub Hn tesCiJ eFmeH nbote mn nakaqarsia nte tesporneia mn na pkaH
rev 17:5 eun ouran mmhsturion shH eJn testeHne Je tbabulwn noC tmaau nmpornos mn nbote mpkaH.
rev 17:6 + auw anau etesHime estaHe ebol Hm pesnoF nnetouaab mn pesnoF nmmntre nihsous. auw nterinau eros airSphre.
rev 17:7 peJaF nai nCi paggelos Je aHrok krSphre anok petnatamok epmh sturion ntesHime mn pequrion etFi Haros etere tsaSFe naph mmoF mn pmht ntap.
rev 17:8 pequrion ntaknau eroF neFSoop pe auw neFSoop an auw Fnhu eHrai Hm pnoun neFbwk eptako auw nserSphre nCi netouhhH HiJm pkaH nai ete nneuran shH an epJwwme mpwnH Jin ntkatabolh mpkosmos eunau epequrion Je neFSoop pe auw neFSoop an auw FnaSwpe
rev 17:9 pai pe pma mpHht ete ountF tsofia auw tsaSFe nape saSF ntoou ne etere tesHime Hmoos eHrai eJwou. auw saSF nrro ne
rev 17:10 pTou auHe poua Soop pkeoua mpatFei auw eFSanei FnaCw noukoui.
rev 17:11 auw pequrion ete neFSoop pe auw tenou neFSoop an ntoF pe pmeH Smoun oua ebol Hm psaSF auw eFna eptako.
rev 17:12 auw pmht ntap ntaknau eroou pmht nrro ne mpatouJi ntmntrro alla eunaJi ouexousia mpequrion.
rev 17:13 nai senarouHht nouwt nseT nteuCom mn teuexousia mpeqhrion.
rev 17:14 nai senamiSe mn peHieib nte peHieib Jro eroou Je pJoeis nenJoeis pe auw prro nnerrwou pe auw netnmmaF nettaHm auw netsotp mpistos.
rev 17:15 - auw peJaF nai Je mmou neiooue ntaknau eroou ere tpolis Hmoos HiJwou nlaos ne mn nefulh mn naspe.
rev 17:16 auw pmht ntap ntaknau eroou mn pequrion nai senameste tpornh nseaas nJaie eskh kaHhu nseouwm nnessarx auw nserwkH mmos Hn oukwHt.

rev 17:18 auw tesHime ntaknau eros te tnoC mpolis ete retmntrmmao nHhts nnrrwou mpkaH.
rev 18:1 = mnnsa nai anau ekeaggelos eFnhu ebol Hn tpe euntF ounoC nexousia auw pkaH aFrouoein ebol Hm peFeoou.
rev 18:2 aFaSkak ebol Hn ounoC nsmh Je asHe nCi tbabulwn noC auw asSwpe mma nouwH nendaimwnion Hi pneuma nim nakaqarton auw mma nSwpe nqurion nim Hi Halht nim.
rev 18:3 Hi akaqarton etbht. Je ebol Hm phrp mpCwnt ntesporneia auHe nCi nHeqnos throu auw nrrwou mpkaH auporneue nmmas auw nmporos mpkaH aurrmmao ebol Hn tCom mpesJhr.
rev 18:4 - auw aiswtm ekesmh ebol Hn tpe esJw mmos Je palaos amou ebol nHhts Je nnetetnkoinonei enesnobe auw nnetnJi ebol Hn nesplugh
rev 18:5 Je anesnobe Jise Sa Hrai etpe auw apnoute rpmeeue nnesJinCons.
rev 18:6 twwbe nas kata nentasaau auw nesHbhue ntetn toobou nas nsepsnau Hm pesJw entaskera mmoF kera nas nsnau
rev 18:7 nesSouSou mn nesJhr ntasSwpe nHhtou Teroou nas nbazanos auw nHhbe. Je esJw mmos Hm pesHht Je anok TnaHmoos an eio nchra oude nTnanau an eHhbe.
rev 18:8 etbe pai Hn ouHoou nouwt senhunCi nesplugh throu pmou auw pHhbe mn pHebwn auw nserokHs Hn oukwHt Je ouJwwre pe pJoeis pnoute etkrine mmos.
rev 18:9 - auw nrrwou mpkaH senarime nseneHpe eHrai eJws nai entauporneue auw auJhr nmmas euSannau epkapnos mpesrwkH
rev 18:10 euaHeratou mpoue etbe qote ntesbazanos euJw mmos Je ouoi ouoi ntnoC mpolis tbabulwn tpolis ettaJrhu Je Hn ouounou nouwt aFei nCi pesHap.
rev 18:11 - nmporos mpkaH senarime nserHhbe eHrai eJws Je mn laau Ce Soop mpeuauaan
rev 18:12 ouauaan nnoub Hi Hat Hi ene mme Hi margariths Hi Sns Hi JhCe Hi sirikon Hi kokkos Hi Se nqinon Hi skeos nim nelefantinon Hi skeos nim nSe eFtaihu Hi Homnt Hi penipe Hi marmaron
rev 18:13 Hi Cinnamomon Hi amomon Hi SouHhne Hi stoi Hi libanos Hi hrp Hi neH Hi samit Hi tbnh Hi esoou Hi Hto Hi maspork Hi Camoul Hi brCoout Hi HmHal.
rev 18:14 auw topora ntoupequmia ntouyuch asbwk auw nounoC ntrufh etnaSwou autako auw nsenaHe eroou an.
rev 18:15 nemporos nai ntaurrmmao nHhts senaaHeratou mpoue etbe qote ntesbazanos eurime auw eurHbbe

rev 18:18 auaSkak ebol eunau epkapnos mpesrwkH euJw mmos Je nim pettntwn eteipolis noC tai ntaurrmmao nHhts nCi narcwn throu.
rev 18:19 auw neuneJ eitn eJn neuaphue euJiSkak ebol eurime eurHhbe euJw mmos Je ouoi ouoi ntnoC mpolis tai ntaurrmmao nHhts nCi neteountau neJhu Hn qallassa ebol Hn tesmntrmmao Je Hn ouounou nouwt asrJaie.
rev 18:20 eufrane tpe eHrai eJws auw netouaab auw napostolos mn neprofuths Je apnoute krine mpetnHap ebol nHhts.
rev 18:21 - auw ouaggelos nJwwre aFFi nounoC nwne nqe nouwne nnout aFnoJF eHrai eqallassa eFJw mmos Je tai te qe etounatauo eHrai Hn ousSne ntbabulwn tnoC mpolis nsetmHe eros.
rev 18:22 auw nCiqarotos Hi mousikon Hi reFJw Hi salpigx nneuswtm eroou nHhte Jin ntenou auw tecniths nim ntecnh nim nneuCntou nHhte Jin ntenou auw nneusetm Hroou mmacanh nHhte Jin ntenou oude smh mpatSeleet Hi Seleet
rev 18:23 oude nneuJere Hhbs nHhte Jin ntenou nnoC nte pkaH neuo neSwt ne Je Hrai Hn noumntreFrpaHre auplana nCi nHeqnos throu.

rev 19:1 = mnnsa nai aiswtm eunoC nsmh nqe noumhhSe enaSwF Hn tpe euJw mmos Je allhlouia. pouJai mn peoou mn tCom mpennoute.
rev 19:2 Je Henme ne auw Hendikaiosunh ne nekHap Je akkrine ntpornh tai ntastake pkaH Hn tesporneia auw aFJi mpekba mpesnoF nneFHmHal ebol Hn nesCiJ.
rev 19:3 auw peJau mpmeHspsnau Je allhlouia. auw peskapnos nhu eHrai Sa eneH neneH
rev 19:4 auw pJoutaFte mpresbeteros aupaHtou mn peFtoou nzwon auouwSt mpnoute etHmoos Hi peqronos euJw mmos Je Hamhn allhlouia.
rev 19:5 = auw aHensmh ei ebol Hm peqronos euJw mmos Je smou epnoute neFHmHal throu etrHote HhtF nkoui mn nnoC.
rev 19:6 auw aiswtm eusmh nqe nounoC mmhhSe auw nqe mpeHroou nHenmoou enaSwou auw nqe ntesmh nHennoC nHroubbai enaSwou euJw mmos Je allhlouia. Je aFrrro Sa eneH neneH nCi pJoeis pennoute ppantwkratwr.

rev 19:8 auw auT nas etresCooles nouSns eFouobS enanouF eFouaab pSns gar ne ndikaiwma nnetouab.
rev 19:9 - auw peJaF nai Je sHai Je naiatou nnentautaHmou epdipnon ntSeleet mpeHieib. peJaF nai Je Henme ne neiSaJe ntaiJoou auw napnoute ne.
rev 19:10 auw aipaHt mpmto ebol nneFourhhte etraouwSt naF auw peJaF nai Je mprCwSt ebol Je ang pekSbhr HmHal mn nekkesnhu nai eneountau tmntmntre nihsous pecristos ouwSt mpnoute tmntmntre gar nis pe pepneuma nte profutia.
rev 19:11 = anau etpe esouhn auw eis ouHto nouobS eumoute epettale eroF Je ppistos auw pme eFnakrine auw neFmiSe Hn oudikaiosunh.
rev 19:12 neFbal de euo nqe nouSaH nkwHt eun oumhhSe nCrhpe HiJn teFaph euntaF ouran eFshH emn laau sooun mmoF eimhti ntoF
rev 19:13 eFCoole nouHoite eFJhC Hn ousnoF auw aumoute epeFran Je pSaJe mpnoute.
rev 19:14 auw neFstrateuma etHn tpe neuouhhH nswF pe eutalhu eHenHto nouobS euCoole nHenSns euouobS auw eutbbhu.
rev 19:15 auw neun oushFe esthm nhu ebol Hn rwF Jekaas Hrai nHhts eFepatasse nenHeqnos throu auw ntoF petnamoone mmoou Hn ouCerwb mpeni pe auw ntoF petnaHwm nteHrwt mphrp ntorgh mpCwnt mpnoute ppantwkratwr.
rev 19:16 eun ouran eFshH eJm peFHoite mn peFmhros Je prro nnerrwou pe auw pJoeis nenJisooue.
rev 19:17 - auw anau ekeaggelos eFaHeratF HiJm prh eFaSkak ebol Hn ounoC nsmh eFJw mmos enHalaate etHhl ntmhhte ntpe Je amHitn swouH eHoun epdipnon noC ntepnoute
rev 19:18 Je etetnaouwm nensarx nnerrwou mn nciliarcos mn nJwwre mn neHtwwr mn netale eroou mn nHmHal mn nrmHe mn nkoui mn nnoC.
rev 19:19 auw anau epequrion mn neFerwou mn peFstrateuma eauswouH eeire noupolemos mn pettalhu epeHto nouobS mn peFstrateuma.
rev 19:20 auw aFCwpe mpequrion mn netnmmaF mn peprofuths nnouJ etnmmaF mn pentaFeire nm maein mpeFmto ebol nai ntaFplana nHhtou nnentauJi mpesHai mpequrion mn nentauouwSt nteFHikwn aunoJou mpesnau euonH eHrai etlumnh nsate etJero Hn ouqhn.
rev 19:21 auw pkeseph aumou Hn tshFe mpettale epeHto tai ntasei ebol Hn teFtapro auw nHalaate throu ausei ebol Hn neusarx.
rev 20:1 = anau euaggelos eFnhu ebol Hn tpe ere nSoSt mpnoun ntootF mn ounoC nHalusis Hn teFCiJ.
rev 20:2 auw aFamaHte mpedrakwn pHoF narcaios ete pai pe pdiabolos psatanas auw aFmorF nSo nrompe
rev 20:3 aFnoJF epesht epnoun aFStam erwF auw aFtwwbe erwF Je nneFplana Ce nenHeqnos Sa nte tSo nrompe. Jwk ebol mnnsa nai senabolF ebol nkekoui nouoeiS.
rev 20:4 - mnnsa nai anau eHenqronos auw auHmoos HiJwou auT nau nouHap auw anau eteyuch nnentaumooutou etbe tmntmntre nihsous auw etbe pSaJe mpnoute auw nete mpououwSt mpequrion mn teFHikwn auw nete mpouJi mpeFmaein eJn teuteHne heJn neuCiJ auwnH auw aurrro mn pecristos nSo nrompe.
rev 20:5 pkeseph de nnetmoout mpouwnH SantouJwk ebol nCi tSo nrompe. tai te tSorp nanastasis.
rev 20:6 naiatF auw Fouaab nCi pete ountF oumeros Hn tSorp nanastasis Je mnte pmeHsnau mmou exousia eHrai eJm pai alla eunaSwpe nouhhb mpnoute mn peFcristos auw senarrro nmmaF ntSo nrompe.
rev 20:7 = Hotan de euSanJwk ebol nCi tSo nrompe senabwl ebol mpsatanas Hn Henmrre
rev 20:8 nFei ebol eplana ntoikoumenh eswouH eHoun ngwg mn magwg ebol Hm peFtoou nkooH mpkaH eHoun eppolumos euo nqe mpSw nqallassa.
rev 20:9 auw auei eHrai eJm ppwCJ mpkaH aukwte etparembolh nnetouaab mn tpolis mpmerit aukwHt ei ebol Hn tpe ebol Hitm pnoute auw aFouomou.
rev 20:10 pdiabolos de etplana mmoou aunoJF etlimnh nkwHt Hi qhn pma ntaunouJ mpequrion eroF mn peprofuths nnouJ auw senabasanize mmoou nteuSh mn peHoou nsetmJimton Sa eneH neneH.
rev 20:11 = anau eunoC nqronos eFouobS auw petHmoos HiJwF apkaH pwt mn tpe HateFHh aFw mpouHe ema nau
rev 20:12 auw anau enetmoout nnoC mn nkoui euaHeratou mpmto ebol mpeqronos auperS HenJwwme ebol auw auouwn nkeJwwme epapwnH pe aukrine nnetmoout ebol Hn netshH enJwwme kata neuHbhue.
rev 20:13 aqallassa Tnnetmoout etnHhts auw pnoun mn amnte auT nnetmoout etnHhtou auw aukrine mpoua poua kata neuHbhue.
rev 20:14 auw pnoun mn amnte aunoJou eHrai etlimnh nsate pai pe pmou mmeHsnau ete tlimnh te nsate.
rev 20:15 auw pete mpouHe eroF eFshH mpJwwme mpwnH aunoJou etlimnh nsate.
rev 21:1 = auw anau eupe nbrre mn oukaH nbrre tSorp gar mpe mn pSorp nkaH auouei ne auw qallassa nesSoop an Ce.
rev 21:2 auw anau etpolis etouaab qierosoluma nbrre esnhu epesht ebol Hn tpe ebol Hitm pnoute essbtwt nqe nouSeleet estamihu mpesHai.
rev 21:3 aiswtm eunoC nsmh ebol Hn tpe esJw mmos Je eis teskunh mpnoute mn nrwme auw FnaouwH nmmau nseSwpe naF nlaos auw ntoF pJoeis neFSwpe nau nnoute
rev 21:4 neFFwte nrmeih nim ebol Hn neubal auw mn mou Ce naSwpe oude Hhbe oude mn aSkak oude mn Hise naSwpe Jin ntenou Je anSorp oueine.
rev 21:5 - auw peJaF nCi petHmoos Hi peqronos Je eis Hhhte Tnatamie nka nim nbrre auw peJaF nai Je sHai Je neiSaJe ntaiJoouse nHot auw Henme ne.
rev 21:6 peJaF nai Je aiSwpe. nalfa auw w peHoueite auw pJwk. anok TnaT mpetobe ebol Hn tpugh mpmoou mpwnH nJinJh.
rev 21:7 petnaJroF naklhronomi nnai auw TnaSwpe naF nnoute neFSwpe nai nShre.
rev 21:8 nCab Hht de ntoou mn napistos mn netbht auw nreFHwtb mn npornos mn nefarmakos auw nrFSmSe eidwlon mn reFJiCol nim ere teutoe naSwpe Hn tlumnh etJero Hn oukwHt mn ouqhn ete pai pe pmou mmeHsnau.
rev 21:9 = auw aFei nCi keoua ebol Hm psaSF naggelos ete ountou tsaSFe mfialh etmeH nneplugh nHah aFSaJe nmmai eFJw mmos Je amou tatsabok etSeleet qim mpeHieib.
rev 21:10 auw aFJit Hm pepneuma eJn outoou noC eFJose aFtsaboi etpolis etouaab qierosoluma esnhu epesht ebol Hn tpe ebol Hitm pnoute
rev 21:11 eountas mmau mpeoou mpnoute ere pesouoein eFeine nouwne mme eFtaihu nqe nouwne niaspis eFeine noukrustalos.
rev 21:12 eun ousobt mmos eFJose eun mntsnoous mpulwn mmos ere mntsnoous naggelos HiJn mpulwn ere Henran shH eros kata nran ntmntsnoous mfulh nenShre mpeisrahl
rev 21:13 ere Somnt mpulwn CwSt epeiebt auw Somnt mpulwn epemHit auw Somnt epemnt auw Somnt eprhs.
rev 21:14 eun mntsnoous nsnte mpsobt ntpolis eushH eroou nCi nran mpmntsnoous napostolos mpeHieib.
rev 21:15 - auw petSaJe nmmai neunoukaS nnoub ntootF nSi Jekaas eFeSi ntpolis mn nespulwn mn pessobt.
rev 21:16 auw tpolis neso ntetragonon ere tesSih ShS mn pesouwSs auw aFSi tpolis mpkaS Sa mntsnoous nSe nstadion nSih auw pesouwSs mn pesJise euShS mn neuerhu.
rev 21:17 auw aFSi pessobt nSe Hm etaFte mmaHe mpSi nourwme ete pai pe ouaggelos.
rev 21:18 auw pessobt eFkht niaspis auw tpolis eskht nnoub enanouF eFeine nouabaChein eFouaab.
rev 21:19 nsnte mpsobt ntpolis eutamihu Hienemme nim tSorp nsnte eseine niaspis tmeHsnte nsappiros tmeHSomte nca rchdwn tmeHFtoe nsmaragdos
rev 21:20 tmeHTe nsardonix tmeHso nsardion tmeHsaSFe ncrusoliqos tmeHSmoune nburullos tmeHyite ntopadion tmeHmhte ncrusoprasos tmeHmntoue nHuaginqinon tmeHmntsnoous namequstos
rev 21:21 auw pmntsnoous mpulwn neuo mmntsnoous mmargariths ere poua poua nmpulwn Soop ebol Hn oumargariths nouwt auw teplatia ntpolis eso nnoub eFouaab nqe nouabaChein eFtbbhu.
rev 21:22 - mpinau de erpe nHhts pJoeis gar pnoute pe pesrpe mn peHieib.
rev 21:23 auw tpolis nesrcria an mprh mn pooH etreurouoein eros peoou gar mpnoute rouoein eros auw pesHhbs pe peHieib.
rev 21:24 auw nHeqnos namooSe ebol Hitm pesouoein mn nrrwou mpkaH eueine mpeueoou eHoun eros
rev 21:25 auw senaSwtm an nnespulwn mpeHoou mn teuSh mn ouSh gar naSwpe mmau
rev 21:26 senaJi eHoun mpeoou mn ptaio nenHeqnos.
rev 21:27 auw nneubwk eHoun eros nCi ouon nim etJaHm mn neteire nenbote mn nreFJiCol ei mhti netshH Hm pJwwme mpeHieib.
rev 22:1 = aFtsaboi eueiero mmoou eFonH eFouobS nqe noukrustalos eFnhu ebol Hm peqronos mpnoute mn peHieib.
rev 22:2 etntmhhte nteplateia ntpolis ere ouShn nwnH Hi peisa mn pai mpeiero eFeire mmntsnoous nkarpos eFT mpeFkarpos Hreebot ereneFCwwbe Soop euqerapia nenHeqnos.
rev 22:3 auw mn laau nbote naSwpe Jin ntenou FnaSwpe de Hrai nHhts nCi peqronos mpnoute mn peHieib auw neFHmHal naSmSe naF
rev 22:4 nsenau epeFHo ere peFran shH eJn teuteHne.
rev 22:5 ntetm ouSh Ce Swpe nsetmrcria Ce mpouoein nenHhbs mn pouoein mprh Je pJoeis pnoute petnarouoein eroou auw nserrro Sa eneH neneH.
rev 22:6 = peJaF nai Je neiSaJe smont auw Henme ne auw pJoeis pnoute nnepneuma nneprofuths aFtauo mmoi peFaggelos etsabe neFHmHal enetnaSwpe. Hn ouCeph.
rev 22:7 eis Hhhte Tnhu tach. naiatF mpetHareH enSaJe nteiprofutia mpeiJwwme.
rev 22:8 - anok Hw iwHannhs petswtm auw etnau enai ntereiswtm auw anau eroou aipaHt etraouwSt mpmto ebol nnourhhte mpaggelos ettsabo mmoi enai.
rev 22:9 auw peJaF nai Je mpwr ang pekSbhr HmHal mn nekkesnhu neprofuths mn netHareH enSaJe mpeiJwwme ouwSt mpnoute.
rev 22:10 auw peJaF nai mprtwwbe nenSaJe nteiprofutia mpeiJwwme Je apeouoeiS gar Hwn eHoun.
rev 22:11 petJinCons mareFJinCons on auw petJaHm mareFJwHm on auw pdikaios mareFrdikaiosunh on auw petouaab mareFtbboF on.
rev 22:12 - eis Hhhte Tnhu Hn ouCeph auw pbeke nmmai eT mpoua poua kata neFHbhue.
rev 22:13 anok pe alfa auw w pSorp auw pHah tarch auw pJwk.
rev 22:14 - naiatou nnentautbbo nneustolh Je ere teuexousia naSwpe eHoun epShn mpwnH auw nsebwk eHoun Hitn mpulh eHoun etpolis.
rev 22:15 senanouJe de ebol nneuHoor mn nefarmakos mn mpornos mn nreFHwtb mn nreFSmSeeidwlon mn ouon nim eteire auw etme mpCol
rev 22:16 - anok ihsous aitnnoou mpaggelos etreFrmntre nhtn nnai Hn nekklhsia. anok pe tnoune auw pgenos ndaueid auw psiou mpnau nHtooue eto nouoein.
rev 22:17 auw pepneuma mn tSeleet seJw mmos Je amou. auw petswtm mareFJoos Je amou. petobe mareFei auw petouwS mareFJimoou nwnH nJinJh.
rev 22:18 - Trmntre ang nouon nim etswtm enSaJe nteiprofhteia mpeiJwwme Je petnaouwH eHrai eJwF pnoute naouwH eHrai eJwF nneplhgh etshH epeiJwwme
rev 22:19 auw petnaFi ebol Hn nSaJe mpJwwme nteiprofhteia pnoute naFi peFmeros ebol Hm pShn mpwnH auw ebol Hn tpolis etouaab nai etshH epeiJwwme.
rev 22:20 - peJaF nCi petrmntre nnai Je se Tnhu Hn ouCeph. amou pJoeis ihsous.
rev 22:21 - tecaris mpenJoeis ihsous mn netouaab throu. Hamhn.
